|            PERFORMANCE COMPARISON: PQC vs Classical          |
+==============================================================+

+------------------------+----------------+----------------+------------+
| Metric                 | Classical MAC  | PQC Signature  | Overhead   |
+------------------------+----------------+----------------+------------+
| Generation Time (avg)  |      16.23 us |     391.73 us |     24.1x |
| Verification Time (avg)|      47.38 us |      85.11 us |      1.8x |
| Authenticator Size     |         16 B   |       3309 B   |    206.8x |
| Generation Throughput  |    61629.5/s  |     2552.8/s  |    24.14x |
| Verify Throughput      |    21106.8/s  |    11748.9/s  |     1.80x |
+------------------------+----------------+----------------+------------+

[ANALYSIS] Analysis:
   - Time Overhead: PQC is 24.1x slower for generation, 1.8x slower for verification
   - Size Overhead: PQC signature is 206.8x larger than MAC
   - Security Benefit: PQC provides quantum resistance
   - Trade-off: Higher computational cost for future-proof security
